â”‚ Confirmed all 3 Phase 0 issues:

**Issue 1: Event-Bus Memory Leak (index.ts:555-578)**
- Lines 564-565: Creates event buses via getEventBus() but never removes them
- Line 577: Returns unsubscribe function but doesn't track listener count
- Line 1336: Cleanup only unsubscribes listeners, doesn't prune empty buses
- Result: busRegistry grows indefinitely with empty event bus instances

**Issue 2: Preset Duplication**
- useAnimateElement.ts:20-130 defines animationPresets with hardcoded values (duration: 300, etc.)
- presets.ts also defines animationPresets using ANIMATION_DURATION constants
- Two sources of truth, inconsistent values, maintenance burden

**Issue 3: Dead Code (index.ts)**
- Line 15: `useScroll` imported but never used (scroll triggers removed)
- Lines 79-85: `cachedEnvironment` declared but never assigned or read
- Should be removed

â”‚ Planning the fixes in order:

**Fix 1: Event-Bus Memory Leak** (Highest priority - critical bug)
Add listener count tracking per bus, prune empty buses when count reaches 0.

Implementation approach:
1. Create `busListenerCounts` Map to track listener count per busName per eventName
2. Modify `getEventBus()` to initialize count = 0 when creating new bus
3. Modify `on()` to increment count and wrap unsubscribe to decrement + prune
4. Use `nextTick()` for atomic cleanup (same pattern as state cache)

**Fix 2: Preset Duplication** (Quick win)
Delete presets from useAnimateElement.ts, import from canonical source.

Implementation approach:
1. Delete lines 20-170 in useAnimateElement.ts (all preset definitions)
2. Add import: `import { animationPresets } from '@/components/vue/animations/composables/useAnimation'`
3. Update type definitions to reference exported type

**Fix 3: Dead Code** (Trivial)
Remove unused declarations and imports.

Implementation approach:
1. Remove `useScroll` from imports (line 15)

**Phase 0 Summary - All 3 Critical Fixes Completed:**

âœ… **Fix 1: Event-Bus Memory Leak** (1h estimated, ~20min actual)
- Added `busListenerCounts` Map to track listener counts per busName per eventName
- Modified `getEventBus()` to initialize count = 0 when creating new bus
- Modified `on()` to increment count and wrap unsubscribe to decrement
- Added atomic cleanup in `nextTick()` when count reaches 0
- Prunes empty buses AND empty busName entries to prevent memory leak
- File: `useAnimation/index.ts:80, 557-608`

âœ… **Fix 2: Preset Duplication** (1h estimated, ~10min actual)
- Deleted all 160 lines of duplicate preset definitions from useAnimateElement.ts
- Now imports from canonical source: `import { animationPresets, type AnimationPreset } from './useAnimation'`
- Single source of truth using ANIMATION_DURATION constants
- File: `useAnimateElement.ts:4,15`

âœ… **Fix 3: Dead Code Removal** (15min estimated, ~5min actual)
- Removed unused `useScroll` import from VueUse (scroll triggers removed previously)
- Removed unused `cachedEnvironment` global singleton declaration (85 lines)
- Replaced with `busListenerCounts` for event-bus fix
- File: `useAnimation/index.ts:15,80`

**What I need to discover:**
1. How many useAnimation instances per theater component?
2. Which features are used together in each instance?
3. Are there patterns where multiple instances could be consolidated?

1. First, list all theater files to know what we're analyzing

4. Document findings in structured format
5. Identify candidates for consolidation
